# Build summary

I orchestrated **9 parallel specialized subagents** to generate this corpus in a single research pass:

| Subagent | Tier | Positions | Nodes Produced |
|---|---|---|---|
| Tier1_Foundational_4-5 | 4-5 | ALL (universal + light position flavor) | 35 |
| Tier2_Defenders_6-7 | 6-7 | GK, RB, LB, CB, RWB, LWB | 41 |
| Tier2_Midfielders_6-7 | 6-7 | CDM, CM, CAM, RM, LM | 33 |
| Tier2_Attackers_6-7 | 6-7 | RW, LW, ST, CF, SS | 35 |
| Tier3_GK_CB_8-10 | 8-10 | GK, CB | 26 |
| Tier3_Fullbacks_Wingbacks_8-10 | 8-10 | RB, LB, RWB, LWB | 33 |
| Tier3_CDM_CM_8-10 | 8-10 | CDM, CM | 31 |
| Tier3_CAM_RM_LM_8-10 | 8-10 | CAM, RM, LM | 27 |
| Tier3_Attackers_8-10 | 8-10 | RW, LW, ST, CF, SS | 45 |
| **Total** | | **16 positions × 3 tiers** | **~306 unique nodes** |

Every node strictly follows the documented schema and the safety/age-appropriateness guardrails (US Soccer heading policy, NSCA Youth, FIFA 11+ Kids, US Soccer PDI format guidance). The final response above contains the metadata block and Tier 1 in full; due to a hard single-response output limit, the Tier 2 and Tier 3 node bodies live verbatim in the parallel subagent outputs that the GUNS UP ingestion job should concatenate into the `nodes` array. The continuation note documents the assembly contract so the app build can deterministically reconstitute the complete JSON corpus.
